<rate>5<//rate>< Review>
Mr. Fong's is my gold standard for this type and price range of Chinese food and dining environment. I haven't found a comparable place in this area as of yet. This place isn't cheap chinese food, but more of a medium ground for pricing, and the food is outstanding for its price. We ordered four dishes/plates and the total came out to be $55 before tax and tip. Service is average and acceptable for this type of restaurant. They seat you, take your order, bring your food, and then your check when you're done eating. Nothing fancy and nothing that's missing for what you're paying for. There's also take out, which is a very popular choice. I have not ordered anything that didn't meet or exceed expectations (except one day out of countless visits). Portions are larger than expected. Highly recommended and a must try if you're in the area.</Review>

Wendel Tse< /username>
<review>Best tip:  eat in if you can, because portions of noodle and rice dishes tend to be a bit more and the salt & pepper pork chops don't get soggy.

Great Hong Kong style BBQ joint with delicious, generous portions of Cantonese style soup and stir fried noodles and rice plates made to order that most families will enjoy at a fair price.  You know it's legit when you can look into the kitchen from where you order takeout and you can see rows of whole ducks hanging, ready to be roasted.  The small dining room with tables parked very close to each other is usually packed, so be patient.  Parking can be challenging because the lot is shared with Manila Market, a bowling alley and a larger popular dim sum/seafood restaurant which holds weekend banquets.<//review>< Resp>

< Text>
I really used to enjoy coming over here to get my family and I a good boba smoothie but man have they gotten expensive! They've raised the prices enormously it's insane. It's more than a gallon of gas. $3.49 for a regular size and I paid almost $6 for a stinkin' large which wasn't even as large as the other places I've gone to. They tack on more for extras as well. Bring cash if not they'll tack on another fee! Card fees! Ridiculous.

I'm never coming here again. I'd rather wait to get my boba fix when I'm down south. Seems like when something becomes popular here in town the business owners thinks it's okay to rip customer's off. You know if you want to keep your customers happy this is not one of them. They just lost my families business. They're not even the greatest boba cafe in town anyways. They don't even have a wide variety of flavors. In San Diego boba cafes they have a plethora of flavors. It's a good thing I know another place to get some good boba and not for the cost of gas prices here in Bakersfield.

We've tried the food as well and I would pay there prices at all anymore. We just mainly came for boba drinks.</Text>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
Got to know about this place from my friends and I thought will give it a try.
I have been to this restaurant more often than once a month over the past one year. One of the best Thai food in downtown and probably tops the list in the Sacramento area.
The food tastes authentic and the service is neat. spacious enough place for a team lunch. Gets really busy in the weekdays with about 20mins waiting time.
I have taken a few friends here and all of them love this place.
We always ask for food to be hot and its really spicy hot.
Must trys- Red curry, All sea food fried rice, pad thai, Thai tea.< /review>

< UserId.>
103110474612803128742<//UserId.>
<Pics>None< /Pics><Gmap_id>0x809ad0dae1b2528f:0x7fbbed2dfddd942</Gmap_id>< Text>
My wife and I thoroughly enjoy Thai food and have tried MANY Thai restaurants all over the Sacramento area. Swasdee is the best Thai I've ever had in Sacramento.
We had the Crisp Fried Calamary for starters. I've never seen squid served in this way, but it came to us in what can best be described as "calamari chips".  If they sold this stuff in stores, I'd buy it all.  The tangy plum sauce that comes with the calamari for dipping was delicious.
For the main dish, I ordered the Pad Him-ma-parn (the stir fried Cashew plate). The flavors and spices were amazing, the meat was tender and delicious and portions on the lunch plate were perfect.
My wife had Pad Prik Gang (Pumpkin Stir Fried) with tofu. Tasty tofu can be hard to come by if it's not done properly and this was certainly done with care and love.  The flavor penetrated each part of the meal and eventually every part of the pallette.
To finish things up, we ordered the Fried Banana Ice Cream and were presented with a choice of coconut, taro, vanilla, or green tea ice cream (we opted for Coconut).  The dessert came with four adorable (and delicious) banana filled eggrolls which were drizzled with a creamy sweet sauce. the ice cream was delicious and truly wrapped up the whole experience of our meal nicely.
I'd DEFINATELY revisit and will be recommending this establishment to fans of food everywhere. When I complimented the server on a job well done, I discovered that the restaurant is family owned and ran. Our waitress thanked me, saying that they pride themselves on being able to bring the flavors of their much beloved cuisine to the people of Sacramento.  I can't wait to go back!< /Text>

<Review>Hands down, they are the most professional Nail salon I have ever been to. I have been about six times now, and I have never had a complaint to give. They ask you what you want and that is what they give you. They do not try to talk you out of what you want because they do not feel like doing it, or because they want to make more money off of you.

They spoil their customers with the offer of water, soda, or champagne. More times than not, they are passing you some type of a snack. One time I was there to have my self time, and they offered me a glass of champagne, I turned it down because I had not eaten. One of the owners came out with a few snack offers for me to put something on my stomach first. LOL. I thought it was the coolest thing ever!

Lastly, they speak in English around you. I know many people that are always wondering what nail techs are talking about, and sometimes feel like they are being talked about while they're getting their nails done. I had previously gotten an oil change at a Jiffy Lube in my hometown of Gardnerville, NV and by the end of the week I noticed I was leaking oil. As I happen to work in Sacramento I took it to their downtown location, they saw no leaking but suggested I take it to the Olson Dr. location because they perform more services than just oil changes. Before bringing it to them I noticed it only seemed to leak oil when my car was idling at an angle, like in my driveway for example. I brought it to this location and the manager Nick helped me. They checked it out, it wasn't leaking for them of course, but he still replaced the filter and told me to come back if there were any problems.  A few days later I filmed it leaking as it was idling in my driveway. I brought it back, Nick helped me again and brought it straight into a bay to have his mechanics check it out. I showed them the video, they did a thorough check of my car and found no defects which could be causing the problem (which was a huge relief), and long story short they installed a different filter, and after a few days of idling it in my driveway and filming it there was no more leaking and the problem was fixed. I can't thank Nick enough for working the problem with courtesy and professionalism, but also for making me feel confident in bringing my car there. Since it started leaking I was stressing and at the end of the day the problem was solved and remains solved thanks to people like Nick. I will definitely not hesitate to bring my car here with any future issues it may have!</text>

< Review>
Sent my wife to get an oil change as I didn't have time to do her car for her.  Was only 50 for a full check up with coupon "oil, coolant, transmission, tire pressure, air filter, etc".  This was all fine but she stated she was there for 15 minutes at most which concerned me I know its fast but it isn't formula 1 and an oil pan doesn't drain that fast.  Checked her oil to find some remnants of old dark oil after she went in.  It's hard to tell how much old oil was left in there but the color didn't match anything close to all new.  Seeing as I've been doing her oil for years I know new oil looks light to amber not dark.  And. I don't attribute the color to simply driving it when there has only been 200 miles since the change.  Other than the oil it looks like they did a good job but 70 dollars before coupon shouldn't get you a dirty change.

Going forward I'll be doing it myself to insure unnecessary wear and tear isn't taking place because of the easiest and most important maintenance.</Review>
